# American Oxford 3000 Flashcards (Direct from PDF)

## Flashcards Set - Page 1

| Front (Word, Level, Group) | Back (Thai Meaning & Example) |
| --- | --- |
| **a, an**<br>Level: A1<br>Group: indefinite article | **หนึ่ง, ตัวหนึ่ง (ใช้กับคำนามทั่วไป)**<br>Example: A student must study hard for the IELTS exam. |
| **abandon**<br>Level: B2<br>Group: v. | **ละทิ้ง, ปล่อย**<br>Example: abandon somebody, The baby had been abandoned by its mother. |
| **ability**<br>Level: A2<br>Group: n. | **ความสามารถ**<br>Example: People with the disease may lose their ability to communicate. |
| **able**<br>Level: A2<br>Group: adj. | **สามารถ**<br>Example: You must be able to speak French for this job. |
| **about**<br>Level: A1<br>Group: prep., adv. | **เกี่ยวกับ, ประมาณ**<br>Example: The lecture was about global warming and its impact on agriculture. |
| **above**<br>Level: A1<br>Group: prep., adv. | **เหนือ, สูงกว่า**<br>Example: The temperature is already above 30 degrees Celsius today. |
| **abroad**<br>Level: B2<br>Group: adv. | **ในต่างประเทศ**<br>Example: to go/travel/live/study abroad  |
| **absolute**<br>Level: B2<br>Group: adj. | **สมบูรณ์, แน่นอน**<br>Example: I've joined a class for absolute beginners. |
| **absolutely**<br>Level: B1<br>Group: adv. | **อย่างแน่นอน, อย่างสิ้นเชิง**<br>Example: You're absolutely right. |
| **academic**<br>Level: B1<br>Group: adj. | **ทางวิชาการ**<br>Example: high/low academic standards |
| **accept**<br>Level: A2<br>Group: v. | **ยอมรับ**<br>Example: He asked me to marry him and I accepted. |
| **acceptable**<br>Level: B2<br>Group: adj. | **ยอมรับได้**<br>Example: Children must learn socially acceptable behaviour. |
| **access**<br>Level: B1<br>Group: n., v. | **การเข้าถึง, เข้าถึง**<br>Example: Students have free access to the university library's online resources. |
| **accident**<br>Level: A2<br>Group: n. | **อุบัติเหตุ**<br>Example: a car/road/traffic accident |
| **accompany**<br>Level: B2<br>Group: v. | **ไปเป็นเพื่อน, ประกอบกับ**<br>Example: accompany somebody/something + adv./prep., His wife accompanied him on the trip. |
| **according to**<br>Level: A2<br>Group: prep. | **ตามที่, อ้างถึง**<br>Example: According to Mick, it's a great movie. |
| **account**<br>Level: B1<br>Group: n. | **บัญชี, บรรยาย**<br>Example: I don't have a bank account. |
| **accurate**<br>Level: B2<br>Group: adj. | **แม่นยำ, ถูกต้อง**<br>Example: an accurate description/picture of something |
| **accuse**<br>Level: B2<br>Group: v. | **กล่าวหา**<br>Example: accuse somebody of something, to accuse somebody of murder/a crime |
| **achieve**<br>Level: A2<br>Group: v. | **บรรลุผล, สำเร็จ**<br>Example: He had finally achieved success. |
| **achievement**<br>Level: B1<br>Group: n. | **ความสำเร็จ**<br>Example: Winning the scholarship was a remarkable achievement for her. |
| **acknowledge**<br>Level: B2<br>Group: v. | **ยอมรับ, ตอบรับ**<br>Example: The government refused to acknowledge the results of the election. |
| **acquire**<br>Level: B2<br>Group: v. | **ได้รับมา, เรียนรู้**<br>Example: Reading daily is an effective way to acquire a large vocabulary. |
| **across**<br>Level: A1<br>Group: prep., adv. | **ข้าม, ฝั่งตรงข้าม**<br>Example: We walked across the bridge to get to the other side of the river. |
| **act**<br>Level: A2<br>Group: v. | **แสดง, กระทำ**<br>Example: The actor acted his part with great skill and emotion. |
| **action**<br>Level: A1<br>Group: n. | **การกระทำ**<br>Example: Immediate action is required to prevent further environmental damage. |
| **active**<br>Level: A2<br>Group: adj. | **คล่องแคล่ว, กระตือรือร้น**<br>Example: He remains active despite his old age by jogging every morning. |
| **activity**<br>Level: A1<br>Group: n. | **กิจกรรม**<br>Example: The school offers a variety of extracurricular activities for students. |
| **actor**<br>Level: A1<br>Group: n. | **นักแสดงชาย**<br>Example: The lead actor delivered a powerful performance in the new movie. |
| **actress**<br>Level: A1<br>Group: n. | **นักแสดงหญิง**<br>Example: She is a talented actress who has won several prestigious awards. |
| **actual**<br>Level: B2<br>Group: adj. | **ตามความเป็นจริง, ที่เกิดขึ้นจริง**<br>Example: The actual cost of the project was much higher than the initial estimate. |
| **actually**<br>Level: A2<br>Group: adv. | **จริงๆ แล้ว**<br>Example: I actually enjoyed the movie more than I thought I would. |
| **ad**<br>Level: B1<br>Group: n. | **การโฆษณา (คำย่อของ advertisement)**<br>Example: I saw an ad for a new smartphone on social media today. |
| **adapt**<br>Level: B2<br>Group: v. | **ปรับตัว, ปรับเปลี่ยน**<br>Example: It can be difficult to adapt to a new culture when living abroad. |
| **add**<br>Level: A1<br>Group: v. | **เพิ่ม, บวก**<br>Example: Please add some sugar to the coffee to make it less bitter. |
| **addition**<br>Level: B1<br>Group: n. | **การเพิ่ม, ส่วนที่เพิ่มเข้ามา**<br>Example: In addition to his salary, he receives a monthly travel allowance. |
| **additional**<br>Level: B2<br>Group: adj. | **เพิ่มเติม**<br>Example: The company decided to hire additional staff to handle the workload. |
| **address**<br>Level: A1<br>Group: n. | **ที่อยู่**<br>Example: Please write your home address clearly on the application form. |
| **adj. A1 ,**<br>Level: A2<br>Group: v. | **ปรับปรุง, ปรับเปลี่ยน**<br>Example: The mechanic had to adjust the car's engine to make it run smoothly. |
| **administration**<br>Level: B1<br>Group: n. | **การบริหาร, การจัดการ**<br>Example: The new administration promised to improve the city's public transport system. |
| **admire**<br>Level: B1<br>Group: v. | **ชื่นชม**<br>Example: I really admire her dedication to helping underprivileged children. |
| **admit**<br>Level: B1<br>Group: v. | **ยอมรับ (ความจริง), อนุญาตให้เข้า**<br>Example: He finally admitted that he had made a mistake in the report. |
| **adopt**<br>Level: B2<br>Group: v. | **รับเลี้ยง, นำมาใช้**<br>Example: The couple decided to adopt a child from a local orphanage. |
| **adult**<br>Level: A1<br>Group: n. | **ผู้ใหญ่**<br>Example: Adults are responsible for their own actions and decisions. |
| **advance**<br>Level: B2<br>Group: n., v., adj. | **ก้าวหน้า, พัฒนาขึ้น**<br>Example: Scientific research has made great advances in medicine recently. |
| **advanced**<br>Level: B1<br>Group: adj. | **ระดับสูง, ก้าวหน้า**<br>Example: This course is designed for students with an advanced level of English. |
| **advantage**<br>Level: A2<br>Group: n. | **ข้อได้เปรียบ, ประโยชน์**<br>Example: One major advantage of living in a city is the convenience of transport. |
| **adventure**<br>Level: A2<br>Group: n. | **การผจญภัย**<br>Example: They went on a hiking adventure in the mountains last summer. |
| **advertise**<br>Level: A2<br>Group: v. | **โฆษณา**<br>Example: Companies spend billions of dollars each year to advertise their products. |
| **advertisement**<br>Level: A2<br>Group: n. | **การโฆษณา**<br>Example: The advertisement for the new car was shown during the football match. |
| **advertising**<br>Level: A2<br>Group: n. | **การโฆษณา (อุตสาหกรรม)**<br>Example: He works in the advertising industry as a creative director. |
| **advice**<br>Level: A1<br>Group: n. | **คำแนะนำ**<br>Example: My teacher gave me some useful advice on how to improve my writing. |
| **advise**<br>Level: B1<br>Group: v. | **แนะนำ**<br>Example: The doctor advised him to quit smoking for the sake of his health. |
| **affair**<br>Level: B2<br>Group: n. | **เหตุการณ์, เรื่องราว**<br>Example: The scandal was a major affair that dominated the news for weeks. |
| **affect**<br>Level: A2<br>Group: v. | **ส่งผลกระทบ**<br>Example: The economic crisis will affect many small businesses in the region. |
| **afford**<br>Level: B1<br>Group: v. | **สามารถจ่ายได้, มีกำลังทรัพย์**<br>Example: Many young people cannot afford to buy their own homes nowadays. |
| **afraid**<br>Level: A1<br>Group: adj. | **กลัว**<br>Example: She is afraid of spiders and always screams when she sees one. |
| **after**<br>Level: A1<br>Group: prep. | **หลังจาก**<br>Example: We went for a walk in the park after finishing our dinner. |
| **afternoon**<br>Level: A1<br>Group: n. | **ตอนบ่าย**<br>Example: I usually feel sleepy in the afternoon after having a heavy lunch. |
| **afterward**<br>Level: B2<br>Group: adv. | **ภายหลัง, หลังจากนั้น**<br>Example: We had dinner first and went to the cinema afterward. |
| **again**<br>Level: A1<br>Group: adv. | **อีกครั้ง**<br>Example: Please try to do the exercise again until you get it right. |
| **against**<br>Level: A2<br>Group: prep. | **ต่อต้าน, กับ**<br>Example: The protest was against the government's new tax policy. |
| **age**<br>Level: A1<br>Group: n. | **อายุ, ยุคสมัย**<br>Example: The average age of students in this class is around 20 years old. |
| **agency**<br>Level: B2<br>Group: n. | **ตัวแทน, หน่วยงาน**<br>Example: She works for an advertising agency. |
| **agenda**<br>Level: B2<br>Group: n. | **วาระการประชุม**<br>Example: The next item on the agenda is the budget for the upcoming project. |
| **agent**<br>Level: B1<br>Group: n. | **ตัวแทน**<br>Example: Our agent in New York deals with all US sales. |
| **aggressive**<br>Level: B2<br>Group: adj. | **ก้าวร้าว**<br>Example: Seals have been known to exhibit aggressive behaviour towards swimmers. |
| **ago**<br>Level: A1<br>Group: adv. | **ที่ผ่านมาแล้ว**<br>Example: two weeks/months/years ago |
| **agree**<br>Level: A1<br>Group: v. | **เห็นด้วย**<br>Example: When he said that, I had to agree. |
| **agreement**<br>Level: B1<br>Group: n. | **ข้อตกลง**<br>Example: an international peace agreement |
| **ah**<br>Level: A2<br>Group: exclam. | **อ้อ, อา (คำอุทาน)**<br>Example: Ah, there you are! |
| **ahead**<br>Level: B1<br>Group: adv. | **ข้างหน้า**<br>Example: I'll run ahead and warn them. |
| **aid**<br>Level: B2<br>Group: n., v. | **ความช่วยเหลือ, ช่วยเหลือ**<br>Example: The organization provides emergency aid to victims of natural disasters. |
| **aim**<br>Level: B1<br>Group: v., n. | **เป้าหมาย, เล็ง**<br>Example: The main aim of this project is to reduce plastic waste in the ocean. |
| **air**<br>Level: A1<br>Group: n. | **อากาศ**<br>Example: Let's go out for some fresh air. |
| **aircraft**<br>Level: B2<br>Group: n. | **เครื่องบิน**<br>Example: fighter/transport/military aircraft |
| **airline**<br>Level: A2<br>Group: n. | **สายการบิน**<br>Example: an airline pilot/passenger |
| **airport**<br>Level: A1<br>Group: n. | **สนามบิน**<br>Example: Gatwick Airport |
| **alarm**<br>Level: B1<br>Group: n. | **สัญญาณเตือนภัย**<br>Example: She decided to sound the alarm (= warn people that the situation was dangerous). |
| **album**<br>Level: B1<br>Group: n. | **อัลบั้ม**<br>Example: a photo album |
| **alcohol**<br>Level: B1<br>Group: n. | **แอลกอฮอล์**<br>Example: He never drinks alcohol. |
| **alcoholic**<br>Level: B1<br>Group: adj. | **ที่มีแอลกอฮอล์**<br>Example: alcoholic drinks/beverages |
| **alive**<br>Level: A2<br>Group: adj. | **มีชีวิตอยู่**<br>Example: Is your mother still alive? |
| **all**<br>Level: A1<br>Group: det., pron. | **ทั้งหมด**<br>Example: All students are required to attend the orientation session tomorrow. |
| **all right**<br>Level: A2<br>Group: adj./adv. | **ตกลง, ไม่เป็นไร**<br>Example: Is everything all right? You look a bit pale today. |
| **allow**<br>Level: A2<br>Group: v. | **อนุญาต**<br>Example: allow somebody/something to do something, His parents won't allow him to stay out late. |
| **almost**<br>Level: A2<br>Group: adv. | **เกือบจะ**<br>Example: I like almost all of them. |
| **alone**<br>Level: A2<br>Group: adj./adv. | **คนเดียว, ตามลำพัง**<br>Example: She prefers to live alone because she enjoys her own company. |
| **along**<br>Level: A2<br>Group: prep., adv. | **ตาม (แนว), ขนานไปกับ**<br>Example: We walked along the beach and enjoyed the beautiful sunset. |
| **already**<br>Level: A2<br>Group: adv. | **แล้ว**<br>Example: ‘Lunch?’ ‘No thanks, I've already eaten.’ |
| **also**<br>Level: A1<br>Group: adv. | **ด้วย, เช่นกัน**<br>Example: She's fluent in French and German. She also speaks a little Italian. |
| **alter**<br>Level: B2<br>Group: v. | **เปลี่ยนแปลง**<br>Example: Prices did not alter significantly during 2019. |
| **alternative**<br>Level: A2<br>Group: n. | **ทางเลือก**<br>Example: The road was closed so we had to find an alternative route. |
| **although**<br>Level: A2<br>Group: conj. | **ถึงแม้ว่า**<br>Example: Although the sun was shining, it wasn't very warm. |
| **always**<br>Level: A1<br>Group: adv. | **เสมอ**<br>Example: There's almost always somebody at home in the evenings. |
| **amazed**<br>Level: B1<br>Group: adj. | **ทึ่ง, ประหลาดใจ**<br>Example: an amazed look |
| **amazing**<br>Level: A1<br>Group: adj. | **น่าทึ่ง**<br>Example: an amazing feat/story/experience |
| **ambition**<br>Level: B1<br>Group: n. | **ความทะเยอทะยาน**<br>Example: She had fulfilled her lifelong ambition. |
| **among**<br>Level: A2<br>Group: prep. | **ท่ามกลาง, ในบรรดา**<br>Example: a house among the trees |
| **amount**<br>Level: A2<br>Group: n. | **จำนวน**<br>Example: I was amazed at the amount he could eat. |
| **analysis**<br>Level: B1<br>Group: n. | **การวิเคราะห์**<br>Example: statistical/data analysis |
| **analyze**<br>Level: A2<br>Group: v. | **วิเคราะห์**<br>Example: Scientists need to analyze the data carefully before drawing conclusions. |
| **ancient**<br>Level: A2<br>Group: adj. | **โบราณ**<br>Example: Archaeologists are excavating the ruined temples of this ancient civilization. |
| **and**<br>Level: A1<br>Group: conj. | **และ**<br>Example: bread and butter |
| **anger**<br>Level: B2<br>Group: n. | **ความโกรธ**<br>Example: She had to find a way to express her pent-up anger. |
| **angle**<br>Level: B2<br>Group: n. | **มุม**<br>Example: a 45° angle |
| **angry**<br>Level: A1<br>Group: adj. | **โกรธ**<br>Example: Her behaviour really made me angry. |
| **animal**<br>Level: A1<br>Group: n. | **สัตว์**<br>Example: the animals and birds of South America |
| **ankle**<br>Level: A2<br>Group: n. | **ข้อเท้า**<br>Example: to sprain/break/twist your ankle |
| **anniversary**<br>Level: B2<br>Group: n. | **วันครบรอบ**<br>Example: on the anniversary of his wife’s death |
| **announce**<br>Level: B1<br>Group: v. | **ประกาศ**<br>Example: announce something, He officially announced his intention to resign at today's press conference. |
| **announcement**<br>Level: B1<br>Group: n. | **การประกาศ**<br>Example: to make an announcement |
| **annoy**<br>Level: B1<br>Group: v. | **ทำให้รำคาญ**<br>Example: annoy somebody, His constant joking was beginning to annoy her. |
| **annoyed**<br>Level: B1<br>Group: adj. | **รู้สึกรำคาญ**<br>Example: annoyed with somebody at/about something, He was beginning to get very annoyed with me about my carelessness. |
| **annoying**<br>Level: B1<br>Group: adj. | **ที่น่ารำคาญ**<br>Example: This interruption is very annoying. |
| **annual**<br>Level: B2<br>Group: adj. | **ประจำปี**<br>Example: an annual meeting/event/report/conference |
| **another**<br>Level: A1<br>Group: det./pron. | **อีกอันหนึ่ง, อื่นๆ**<br>Example: I'm still hungry, can I have another slice of pizza, please? |
| **answer**<br>Level: A1<br>Group: n., v. | **คำตอบ, ตอบ**<br>Example: She couldn't find the answer to the last question on the test. |
| **anxious**<br>Level: B2<br>Group: adj. | **วิตกกังวล**<br>Example: The bus was late and Sue began to get anxious. |
| **any**<br>Level: A1<br>Group: det., pron. | **บ้าง, ใดๆ**<br>Example: Do you have any suggestions on how we can improve our service? |
| **anybody**<br>Level: A2<br>Group: pron. | **ใครก็ตาม**<br>Example: Is there anybody who can help me? |
| **anymore**<br>Level: A2<br>Group: adv. | **อีกต่อไป (ใช้ในประโยคปฏิเสธ)**<br>Example: He doesn't live here anymore; he moved to London last year. |
| **anyone**<br>Level: A1<br>Group: pron. | **ใครก็ได้, ใครก็ตาม**<br>Example: Is anyone there? |
| **anything**<br>Level: A1<br>Group: pron. | **อะไรก็ตาม, อะไรก็ได้**<br>Example: Would you like anything else? |
| **anyway**<br>Level: A2<br>Group: adv. | **อย่างไรก็ตาม**<br>Example: It's too expensive and anyway the colour doesn't suit you. |
| **anywhere**<br>Level: A2<br>Group: adv., pron. | **ทุกที่, ที่ไหนก็ได้**<br>Example: I've lost my keys and I can't find them anywhere in the house. |
| **apart**<br>Level: B1<br>Group: adv. | **แยกกัน, ห่างกัน**<br>Example: The two houses stood 500 metres apart. |
| **apartment**<br>Level: A1<br>Group: n. | **ห้องชุด, อพาร์ตเมนต์**<br>Example: They rented a small apartment in the city center to be close to work. |
| **apologize**<br>Level: B1<br>Group: v. | **ขอโทษ**<br>Example: Why should I apologize? |
| **app**<br>Level: A2<br>Group: n. | **แอปพลิเคชัน**<br>Example: You first need to install the app on your device. |
| **apparent**<br>Level: B2<br>Group: adj. | **ที่เห็นได้ชัด**<br>Example: Their devotion was apparent. |
| **apparently**<br>Level: B2<br>Group: adv. | **ตามที่เห็น, ดูเหมือนว่า**<br>Example: Apparently they are getting divorced soon. |
| **appeal**<br>Level: B2<br>Group: n., v. | **ดึงดูด, อุทธรณ์**<br>Example: The new design of the car appeals to younger customers. |
| **appear**<br>Level: A2<br>Group: v. | **ปรากฏตัว**<br>Example: Three days later a rash appeared. |
| **appearance**<br>Level: A2<br>Group: n. | **รูปลักษณ์**<br>Example: the physical/outward/external appearance of something |
| **apple**<br>Level: A1<br>Group: n. | **แอปเปิ้ล**<br>Example: Peel and core the apples. |
| **application**<br>Level: B1<br>Group: n. | **การสมัคร, แอปพลิเคชัน**<br>Example: a planning/patent/visa application |
| **apply**<br>Level: A2<br>Group: v. | **สมัคร, นำมาใช้**<br>Example: You should apply in person/by letter. |
| **appointment**<br>Level: B1<br>Group: n. | **การนัดหมาย**<br>Example: I've got a dental appointment at 3 o'clock. |
| **appreciate**<br>Level: B1<br>Group: v. | **ซาบซึ้ง, เห็นคุณค่า**<br>Example: Over the years he came to appreciate the beauty and tranquillity of the river. |
| **approach**<br>Level: B2<br>Group: n., v. | **วิธีการ, เข้าใกล้**<br>Example: We need to find a new approach to solve this complex problem. |
| **appropriate**<br>Level: B2<br>Group: adj. | **เหมาะสม**<br>Example: an appropriate response/measure/method |
| **approval**<br>Level: B2<br>Group: n. | **การอนุมัติ, ความเห็นชอบ**<br>Example: She desperately wanted to win her father's approval. |
| **approve**<br>Level: B2<br>Group: v. | **อนุมัติ, เห็นชอบ**<br>Example: I told my mother I wanted to leave school but she didn't approve. |
| **approximately**<br>Level: B1<br>Group: adv. | **โดยประมาณ**<br>Example: The journey took approximately seven hours. |
| **April**<br>Level: A1<br>Group: n. | **เมษายน**<br>Example: in April, She was born in April. |
| **architect**<br>Level: A2<br>Group: n. | **สถาปนิก**<br>Example: The house was designed by architect Louis Kahn. |
| **architecture**<br>Level: A2<br>Group: n. | **สถาปัตยกรรม**<br>Example: to study architecture |

## Flashcards Set - Page 2

| Front (Word, Level, Group) | Back (Thai Meaning & Example) |
| --- | --- |
| **bomb**<br>Level: B1<br>Group: n., v. | **ระเบิด**<br>Example: The bomb disposal squad was called in to neutralize the suspicious package. |
| **bond**<br>Level: B2<br>Group: n. | **ข้อผูกมัด, พันธะ**<br>Example: the bond that links us |
| **bone**<br>Level: A2<br>Group: n. | **กระดูก**<br>Example: He survived the accident with no broken bones. |
| **book**<br>Level: A1<br>Group: n. | **หนังสือ, จอง**<br>Example: His desk was covered with piles of books. |
| **boot**<br>Level: A1<br>Group: n. | **รองเท้าบูท**<br>Example: (British English), walking boots |

| **nation**<br>Level: B1<br>Group: n. | **ประเทศ, ชนบท**<br>Example: European/Arab/Asian nations |
| **national**<br>Level: A2<br>Group: adj. | **ระดับชาติ**<br>Example: The government announced a new national policy to improve the public education system. |
| **native**<br>Level: B1<br>Group: adj., n. | **พื้นเมือง, ของท้องถิ่น**<br>Example: She is a native speaker of English who also speaks fluent French and Spanish. |
| **natural**<br>Level: A1<br>Group: adj. | **เป็นธรรมชาติ**<br>Example: the natural world (= of trees, rivers, animals and birds) |
| **naturally**<br>Level: B1<br>Group: adv. | **โดยธรรมชาติ**<br>Example: Naturally, I get upset when things go wrong. |

| **nearly**<br>Level: A2<br>Group: adv. | **เกือบจะ**<br>Example: The bottle's nearly empty. |

| **necessarily**<br>Level: B1<br>Group: adv. | **อย่างจำเป็น**<br>Example: The number of places available is necessarily limited. |

| **neck**<br>Level: A2<br>Group: n. | **คอ**<br>Example: He tied a scarf around his neck. |

| --- | --- |
| **race (of people)**<br>Level: B1<br>Group: n. | **เชื้อชาติ, เผ่าพันธุ์**<br>Example: Discrimination based on race or religion is strictly prohibited by the law. |

| **them**<br>Level: A1<br>Group: pron. | **พวกเขา (กรรม)**<br>Example: I saw them in the park yesterday. |
| **theme**<br>Level: B1<br>Group: n. | **แนวคิดหลัก, หัวข้อ**<br>Example: The theme of the conference is "Sustainable Development". |
| **themselves**<br>Level: A2<br>Group: pron. | **พวกเขาเอง**<br>Example: They built the house themselves. |
| **then**<br>Level: A1<br>Group: adv. | **ตอนนั้น, จากนั้น**<br>Example: Ill see you then. |

| **therapy**<br>Level: B2<br>Group: n. | **การบำบัด**<br>Example: She is undergoing physical therapy after her accident. |

| **therefore**<br>Level: B1<br>Group: adv. | **ดังนั้น**<br>Example: He's only 17 and therefore not eligible to vote. |

| **youth**<br>Level: B1<br>Group: n. | **วัยเยาว์**<br>Example: in somebody's youth, He had been a talented musician in his youth. |
| **zero**<br>Level: A2<br>Group: number | **ศูนย์**<br>Example: Five, four, three, two, one, zero… We have lift-off. |
| **zone**<br>Level: B2<br>Group: n. | **เขต / โซน**<br>Example: a war/combat/demilitarized/exclusion zone |
